force (fooris) n. 1 awood; xoog; quwad. e.g. The force of the flood water broke the gate. 2 quwad lagu caabbiyo qof ama shay. e.g. The police used force to inter into the house. 3 awood qof ka fakarisa ama ku khasabta in uu ficil sameeyo. e.g. The force of logic opinion. 4 dhaqangalyo; bilaabasho. e.g. The new rule come into force in this month. 5 ciidan abaabulan. e.g. Peacekeep ing force. 6 forces, askar; ciidan hubaysan. e.g. Enemy forces. 7 dad loo abaabulay in ay wax gaar ah ka wada shaqeeyaan. e.g. Legal forces.

-v., forced, forcing. 1 khasbid; maquunin {al-zama}. e.g. We should have to force him to leave. The brutal civil war forced us to fled. 2 xoog ku furid ama ku jabin. e.g. He forced the door. 3 xoog adeegsad; ku cariirin ama ku maroojin. e.g. She forced her feet into a new shoes. 4 xoog ama khasab u keenind. e.g. The unhappy wife forced to smile. 5 kufsad; qabsad; xoogid, siiba qof dumar ah.

-by force of, ku maquunin ama ku dirqin xoog. e.g. Using power by force of arms.

-by main force, awood buuxda isticmaalid. e.g. The US conquered Iraq by main force.

-force someone’s hand, ku qaadid qof in uu wax sameeyo.

franchise (‘faraan,jaayz) n. 1 ogolaansho dawlad ama shirkad qof ama koox u siiso in ay wax gaar ah ka ganacsan karaan, sida in ay warbaahin furan karaan ama shirkad alaabteed gadi karaan. 2 ganacsi hab noocaan ah ku furan. 3 ogolaansho la siiyo urur in uu yeelan koro koox cayaartoy. 4 [usu.franchise player] cayaartoy u cayaara naadi. 5 [usu. the franchise] xuquuqda lagu codayn karo ama afti lagu dhiiban karo. 6 xuquuda waddani.

-v. siin ogalaansho. e.g. A franchised restaurant. -franchi see (,faraan,jaay’zi) n.; -franchiser or franchisor (,faraanja’zoor) n.

francium (‘faraansiyam) n. curiye kiimiko: astaan Fr; tiro atomic, 87; culays atomic, 223.

-n. astaan rasmi ah oo ku taal shay ladirayo oo aan looga baahnayn bixinta tigit. -franker n.

fratricide (‘faraatra,saaydh) v. 1 dilid qof walaalkiis ama walaashiis. 2 qof dila walaalkiis ama walaashis. 3 ku dil kama, siiba qof ciidankiis dilo.

fraud (faroodh) n. 1 ficil lagu sameeyo tuugo, sir, been, dhac, ama xatooyo si loo sad-bursado. e.g. Several So malis were convicted of fraud. 2 qof dadka sira ama dhaca oo aan ahayn waxa uu sheeganayo. e.g. As a com munity leader, he’s an absolute fraud.

fraudulent (‘faroojalanti) adj. 1 lagu helay, lagu sameeyay, ama la xiriira laqdabo, siiba mid danbi leh. e.g. A fraudu lent car dealer. 2 been ama booli ku maalaysi. -fraudu lence n.; -fraudulently adv.

fraught (faroot) adj. fraught with, xaalad dhibaato leh ama keenta. e.g. A refugee’s life is fraught with hardships. A civil war is a fraught with horror.

fray1 (farey) v. 1 tifmid ama dun-go’id, siiba xarig ama maro; diin-diimid ama duf-rifmid. e.g. His old shirt was frayed the collar. [as adj. frayed] e.g. The frayed collar of his old shirt. 2 xumaatin ama siidarsad. e.g. The hard work frayed his nerves. 3 ku-rifid ama ku-xoqid dhirta, siiba lab ugaareed marka geeso u soo baxayaan ama xilliga orgoodka (the rut)

fray2 n. muran ama dagaal. e.g. The warlords were involved in the fray.

frazzle (‘faraazal) v. -zled, -zling. 1 daalid; dhacsaalid. e.g. A frazzled mother. 2 tifmid; dhammaatin. e.g. The sleeves of his coat were frazzled.

futurist (‘fuyuujaristi) n. 1 qof barta waxa imaandoona kana diga ayada oo lagu saleeyay waxa joogtada ah. 2 qof aaminsan aakhirada.

-adj. la xiriira waxa imaandoona, siiba horumarka sancada. futuristic (,fuyuuja’ristik) adj. la xiriira ama ahba sancada cusub. e.g. Futuristic design. -futuristically adv. futurology (,fuyuuja’raalaji) n. hab lagu saadaaliyo horumarka sancada iyo cilimiga saayniska (science) sida ay u saamayn doonaan bulshada. -futurological adj.; - futurologist n.

futz (fatis) v. 1 [informal] waqti-dhumin; qof ku mashquula wax aan lahayn macne. e.g. He futzed around in the office. 2 futz around with, wax ku cayaarid ahaan loo sameeyo.

fuzz1 (faz) n. 1 baabul; timo ama dhogor jilicsan oo kacasan. e.g. A fuzzy hair. 2 caweero; muuqaal ciiro ku jirto. fuzz2 n. [informal] the fuzz, the police (askari). fuzzy (‘fazi) adj. fuzzier, fuzziest. 1 timo ama dhogor jilcsan leh. e.g. A young girl with a fuzzy hair. 2 caweero leh ama ciiro ku jirto; aan la fahmi karin ama aan caddayn. e.g. This photograph is very fuzzy. -fuzziness n. fuzzy-wuzzy (‘fazi ‘wazi) n., pl. -ies. [British informal] qof madow oo timo jareer ah leh.

FWB abbr. four-wheel brake.

SMALI-ABWAANARY: Second Edition

426

FWD gadolinium

FWD abbr. 1 four-wheel drive. 2 front-wheel drive. fwd. abbr. forward.

F-word n. [informal] maldahaad erayga “fuck.” FY abbr. fiscal year.

-fy dibgale (suffix) macnihiisu yahay: ka dhigid ama noqday. e.g. Purify = nadiifin. Simplify = sahlid.

FYI abbr. for your information (si laguu wargaliyo ama si aad ula socodotid).

fyke or fyke net (faayk) n. shabaq danbiil u eg oo lagu dabo kalluun.

Gg

G1 or g (jii) n., pl. Gs or G’s 1 xarafka todobaad ee alifba’da English ka. 2 xarafka ku xiga F ee tiro isdabayaal ah. e.g. Row G in a parking lot.

G2 astaan (symbol) general audiences (filim ay daawan karto da’ kasta).

g abbr. 1 Chemistry gas. 2 gram (s). 3 karaar (acceleration) uu keeno cuf-jiidadka dhulka (gravity) oo la mid ah 9.81 m s-2.

G8 abbr. Siddeedda Kooxood (Group of Eight). GA abbr. 1 General Assembly. 2 general aviation. 3 Gen eral of the Army. 4 Georgia (oo loo qoro hab boosteedka). Ga (gaa) astaan curiye gallium.

Ga. abbr. Georgia.

gab (gaab) v. gabbed, gabbing. [informal] hadlid in badan; sheekaysad dheer. e.g. They were gabbing all day on the phone. We gabbed for hours about Somalia.

-n. hadal ama sheekaysi dheer.

gabble (‘gaabal) v. daldalid, siiba hadal; tartarid {tarthara}. e.g. He gabbled unrecognizable language. They were gabbling all night.

-n. hadal boobto ama dhawaaq ah; yabaq ama gunuunuc. e.g. I can’t study with all that gabble in the room. - gabbler n.

gabby (‘gaabi) adj. gabbier, gabbiest. [informal] war badni; hadaltiro {jamluun}.

gable (‘geybal) n. gidaar qaybtiis saddex-xagal u eg oo saqafku ka kala rogmado.

gable roof n. saqaf kala rogan.

Gabon (gaa’boon) waddan ku yaal Galbeedka Afrika ee xeebaha Badda Atlantic-ka; darisna la ah Cameroon, Republic of the Congo, iyo Equatorial Guinea; caasimad, Libreville; luuqad, French.

 Gabon

Gaboon viper n. mas sun leh oo dheer, lagana holo Afrika. Gaborone (,gaaba’ruuney) magaala madaxda Botswana. Gabriel (‘geybriyal) n. Malagga Jabriil oo soo gaarsiiyay Qur’aanka Nabi Muhammad (csw).

gad (gaadh) v. gadded, gadding. [informal] qarraafid; wareegid; hadba meel tagid. e.g. He gadded about all night, looking for pleasure.

gadabout (‘gaadha,bawt) n. qof joogto u qarraafa ama u raaxo doonta.

gadfly (‘gaadh,falaay) n., pl. -flies. 1 dhuug; diqsi wayn oo xoolaha qaniina, siiba geela iyo fardaha. 2 qof kadka kale dura oo ka caraysiiya ama ka dagaaliya.

gadget (‘gaajit) n. qalab yar oo wax lagu farsameeyo. e.g. Clippers and a can opener are small gadgets. -gadge teer n.; -gadgetry n.; -gadgetry adj.

gadolinium (,gaadhal’iniyam) n. curiye kiimiko oo ah bir danbasi ah oo jilicsan: astaan Gd; tiro atomic, 64; culays atomic, 157.25.
